    [Height] decimal(18,2) NOT NULL,

    [cod_currency] nvarchar(3) NOT NULL,
    [ShippingFee] decimal(18,2) NOT NULL,

    [TotalFee] decimal(18,2) NOT NULL,

    [Notes] nvarchar(max) NULL,
    [CreatedAt] datetime2 NOT NULL,
    [UpdatedAt] datetime2 NULL,
    [IsDeleted] bit NOT NULL,
    [RowVersion] rowversion NULL,
    CONSTRAINT [PK_parcels] PRIMARY KEY ([Id]),
    CONSTRAINT [FK_parcels_hubs_CurrentHubId] FOREIGN KEY ([CurrentHubId]) REFERENCES [hubs] ([Id]) ON DELETE NO ACTION,

FROM [sys].[default_constraints] [d]
